//   "global using Alias = Type" KHÃNG háŧ tráŧĢ type-arguments (e.g. Alias<T>)
//   â KHÃNG dÃđng kiáŧu ÄÃģ. Cháŧ import namespace bÃŽnh thÆ°áŧng nhÆ° bÃŠn dÆ°áŧi.
//
// Nháŧ dÃēng nÃ y, máŧi file trong project Äáŧu dÃđng ÄÆ°áŧĢc Task<T>

========================================
--- FILE: WorkflowConstants.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Constants
{
    public static class WorkflowConstants
    {
        public static string GetStatusName(int id) => id switch
        {
            1 => "CREATED",
            2 => "ASSIGNED",
            3 => "IN-PROGRESS",
            4 => "FAILED",
            5 => "REVIEW-1",
            6 => "REVIEW-2",
            7 => "APPROVED",
            8 => "IN-TEST",
            9 => "RESOLVED",
            10 => "CLOSED",
            _ => $"STATUS-{id}"
        };

        public static string GetPriorityName(int id) => id switch
        {
            4 => "Critical",
            3 => "High",
            2 => "Medium",
            1 => "Low",
            _ => "Unknown"
        };
    }
}

--- FILE: AuthDTOs.cs ---

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs
{
    // =====================================================
    // DTO (Data Transfer Object) â Äáŧi tÆ°áŧĢng truyáŧn dáŧŊ liáŧu giáŧŊa cÃĄc táš§ng
    //
    // TášĄi sao cáš§n DTO thay vÃŽ truyáŧn Entity thášģng?
    //   Entity cháŧĐa tášĨt cášĢ cáŧt DB (káŧ cášĢ PasswordHash, CreatedAt...)
    //   DTO cháŧ cháŧĐa ÄÃšng dáŧŊ liáŧu táš§ng trÃŠn cáš§n biášŋt
    //   â an toÃ n hÆĄn, giášĢm coupling giáŧŊa táš§ng
    // =====================================================

    /// <summary>
    /// Kášŋt quášĢ trášĢ váŧ sau khi gáŧi IAuthService.LoginAsync().
    ///
    /// DÃđng Result Pattern thay vÃŽ throw Exception cho láŧi nghiáŧp váŧĨ:
    ///   - Form dáŧ kiáŧm tra: if (!result.Success) { lblError.Text = result.ErrorMessage; }
    ///   - KhÃīng cáš§n try-catch cho láŧi "sai máš­t khášĐu" (ÄÃĒy khÃīng phášĢi exception)
    ///   - Exception cháŧ dÃ nh cho láŧi hášĄ táš§ng (DB mášĨt kášŋt náŧi, ...)
    /// </summary>
    public class LoginResult
    {
        public bool   Success      { get; init; }
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; init; } // null khi thÃ nh cÃīng
        public UserSessionDto? User { get; init; } // null khi thášĨt bášĄi

        // Factory methods â tášĄo kášŋt quášĢ rÃĩ nghÄĐa, khÃīng new tráŧąc tiášŋp
        public static LoginResult Ok(UserSessionDto user)
            => new() { Success = true, User = user };

        public static LoginResult Fail(string message)
            => new() { Success = false, ErrorMessage = message };
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// ThÃīng tin user cáš§n thiášŋt sau khi ÄÄng nháš­p â lÆ°u vÃ o AppSession.
    ///
    /// Cháŧ§ Äáŧng KHÃNG cÃģ PasswordHash Äáŧ:
    ///   - KhÃīng vÃī tÃŽnh láŧ hash ra Form/UI
    ///   - GiášĢm dáŧŊ liáŧu khÃīng cáš§n thiášŋt trong báŧ nháŧ
    /// </summary>
    public class UserSessionDto
    {
        public int    Id         { get; init; }
        public string Username   { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string FullName   { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string Email      { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string? AvatarPath { get; init; }

        // Danh sÃĄch tÃŠn role: ["Admin"], ["Manager"], ["Developer"]
        // DÃđng Äáŧ kiáŧm tra quyáŧn trong AppSession (IsAdmin, IsManager...)
        public List<string> Roles { get; init; } = new();
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    public class Attachment
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        [Required, MaxLength(255)]
        public string FileName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [Required, MaxLength(500)]
        public string FilePath { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(100)]
        public string? ContentType { get; set; }

        public long FileSizeBytes { get; set; }

        public DateTime UploadedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        public int TaskItemId { get; set; }
        public TaskItem TaskItem { get; set; } = null!;

        public int UploadedById { get; set; }
        public User UploadedBy { get; set; } = null!;
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities

    /// <summary>
    /// KhÃĄch hÃ ng - ÄÆĄn váŧ yÃŠu cáš§u phÃĄt triáŧn dáŧą ÃĄn

    /// </summary>
    public class Expense
    {

        public int ProjectId { get; set; }
        public Project Project { get; set; } = null!;

        [Required, MaxLength(100)]

        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(18,2)")]
        public decimal Amount { get; set; }

    {

========================================
--- FILE: Project.cs ---
========================================

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.Schema;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    public class Project
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(2000)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        // ---- KhÃĄch hÃ ng ----
        public int? CustomerId { get; set; }
        public Customer? Customer { get; set; }

        // ---- NgÆ°áŧi sáŧ háŧŊu / PM ----
        public int OwnerId { get; set; }
        public User Owner { get; set; } = null!;

        // ---- Timeline ----
        public DateOnly StartDate { get; set; }
        public DateOnly? PlannedEndDate { get; set; }
        public DateOnly? ActualEndDate { get; set; }

        // ---- NgÃĒn sÃĄch ----
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(18,2)")]
        public decimal Budget { get; set; } = 0;

        // ---- TrášĄng thÃĄi & ÆŊu tiÃŠn ----
        /// <summary>NotStarted | InProgress | OnHold | Completed | Cancelled</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(30)]
        public string Status { get; set; } = "NotStarted";

        /// <summary>1=Low | 2=Medium | 3=High | 4=Critical</summary>
        public byte Priority { get; set; } = 2;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        public DateTime UpdatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();
        public ICollection<ProjectMember> Members { get; set; } = new List<ProjectMember>();
        public ICollection<Expense> Expenses { get; set; } = new List<Expense>();

        /* ================= COMPUTED (khÃīng map DB) ================= */
        [NotMapped]
        public decimal TotalExpense => Expenses?.Sum(e => e.Amount) ?? 0;

        [NotMapped]
        public int ProgressPercent
        {
            get
            {
                var rootTasks = Tasks?.Where(t => t.ParentTaskId == null).ToList();
                if (rootTasks == null || rootTasks.Count == 0) return 0;
                return (int)rootTasks.Average(t => t.ProgressPercent);
            }
        }
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities

    /// <summary>
    /// TrášĄng thÃĄi cÃīng viáŧc â workflow 10 bÆ°áŧc quášĢn lÃ― dáŧą ÃĄn pháš§n máŧm.
    ///

    /// Luáŧng reject:

    /// </summary>
    public class Status
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TÃŠn trášĄng thÃĄi (VD: CREATED, IN-PROGRESS, REVIEW-1...).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(50)]
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>MÃī tášĢ cÃīng dáŧĨng cáŧ§a trášĄng thÃĄi (hiáŧn tháŧ trÃŠn UI).</summary>
        [MaxLength(300)]

        /// <summary>TháŧĐ táŧą hiáŧn tháŧ trÃŠn Kanban / danh sÃĄch (0 = Äáš§u tiÃŠn).</summary>
        public byte DisplayOrder { get; set; } = 0;

        /// <summary>MÃĢ mÃ u hex Äáŧ tÃī mÃ u trÃŠn giao diáŧn (VD: #4CAF50).</summary>
        [MaxLength(7)]
        public string? ColorHex { get; set; }

        public ICollection<TaskItem> TaskItems { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();
    }

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.Schema;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// CÃīng viáŧc (Task) trong dáŧą ÃĄn.
    /// 
    /// Workflow 10 trášĄng thÃĄi:
    ///   CREATED â ASSIGNED â IN-PROGRESS â REVIEW-1 â REVIEW-2 â APPROVED â IN-TEST â RESOLVED â CLOSED
    ///                             â             â          â                     â
    ///                             âââââââââ FAILED âââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
    /// 
    /// Máŧi giai ÄoášĄn cÃģ ngÆ°áŧi pháŧĨ trÃĄch riÃŠng:
    ///   - AssignedTo: ngÆ°áŧi lÃ m task (Developer)
    ///   - Reviewer1: ngÆ°áŧi review láš§n 1 (peer/team lead)
    ///   - Reviewer2: ngÆ°áŧi review láš§n 2 (senior/architect)
    ///   - Tester: ngÆ°áŧi kiáŧm tháŧ­ (QA)
    /// 
    /// Luáŧng gÃĄn ngÆ°áŧi:
    ///   TášĄo task â gÃĄn Assignee
    ///   Assignee xong â chuyáŧn REVIEW-1 + gÃĄn Reviewer1
    ///   Reviewer1 pass â chuyáŧn REVIEW-2 + gÃĄn Reviewer2
    ///   Reviewer2 pass â APPROVED â IN-TEST + gÃĄn Tester
    ///   BášĨt káŧģ ai (Reviewer1/2, Tester) reject â FAILED â Assignee sáŧ­a lášĄi
    /// </summary>
    public class TaskItem
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TiÃŠu Äáŧ cÃīng viáŧc (bášŊt buáŧc, táŧi Äa 200 kÃ― táŧą).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>MÃī tášĢ chi tiášŋt cÃīng viáŧc (tÃđy cháŧn, táŧi Äa 2000 kÃ― táŧą).</summary>
        [MaxLength(2000)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        /// <summary>ÄÃĄnh dášĨu task ÄÃĢ hoÃ n thÃ nh (táŧą Äáŧng set khi ProgressPercent = 100).</summary>
        public bool IsCompleted { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Pháš§n trÄm hoÃ n thÃ nh: 0â100. Khi = 100 â IsCompleted = true.</summary>
        [Range(0, 100)]
        public byte ProgressPercent { get; set; } = 0;

        /// <summary>Sáŧ giáŧ Æ°áŧc tÃ­nh Äáŧ hoÃ n thÃ nh task.</summary>
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(6,1)")]
        public decimal? EstimatedHours { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Sáŧ giáŧ tháŧąc tášŋ ÄÃĢ lÃ m.</summary>
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(6,1)")]
        public decimal? ActualHours { get; set; }

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
        public DateTime UpdatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        /// <summary>HášĄn chÃģt hoÃ n thÃ nh task.</summary>
        public DateTime? DueDate { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Tháŧi Äiáŧm task ÄÆ°áŧĢc ÄÃĄnh dášĨu hoÃ n thÃ nh (status = RESOLVED/CLOSED).</summary>

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// TÃ i khoášĢn ngÆ°áŧi dÃđng trong háŧ tháŧng.
    /// Máŧt user cÃģ tháŧ ÄÃģng nhiáŧu vai trÃē trÃŠn task: Assignee, Reviewer, Tester.
    /// </summary>
    public class User
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TÃŠn ÄÄng nháš­p (unique, dÃđng lÃ m khÃģa nghiáŧp váŧĨ).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(50)]
        public string Username { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Háŧ vÃ  tÃŠn Äáš§y Äáŧ§.</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string FullName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Email (unique).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Máš­t khášĐu ÄÃĢ hash bášąng BCrypt (WorkFactor 12).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(256)]
        public string PasswordHash { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(20)]
        public string? Phone { get; set; }

        [MaxLength(255)]

        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
        public DateTime? LastLogin { get; set; }

        public ICollection<TaskItem> AssignedTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        // ââ GD3: Workflow Review & Test âââââââââââââââââââââââ

========================================
--- FILE: PasswordHelper.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Táš­p trung logic hash/verify máš­t khášĐu bášąng BCrypt.
    ///
    /// TášĄi sao BCrypt thay vÃŽ SHA-256?
    ///   SHA-256: thuáš­t toÃĄn hash nhanh, GPU cÃģ tháŧ tháŧ­ 10 táŧ· hash/giÃĒy â dáŧ brute-force
    ///   BCrypt:  cáŧ tÃŽnh cháš­m (~300ms/hash), cÃģ cost factor Äiáŧu cháŧnh ÄÆ°áŧĢc
    ///            táŧą sinh salt ngášŦu nhiÃŠn cho máŧi password â cháŧng rainbow table
    ///
    /// TášĄi sao tÃĄch ra Helper riÃŠng?
    ///   AuthService vÃ  UserService Äáŧu cáš§n hash/verify
    ///   â Äáš·t 1 cháŧ trÃĄnh duplicate code, dáŧ Äáŧi thuáš­t toÃĄn sau nÃ y
    /// </summary>
    public static class PasswordHelper
    {
        // WorkFactor 12 = 2^12 = 4096 vÃēng láš·p náŧi báŧ â ~300ms trÃŠn CPU thÃīng thÆ°áŧng
        // TÄng lÃŠn 13-14 nášŋu server mášĄnh hÆĄn (máŧi +1 tÄng gášĨp ÄÃīi tháŧi gian hash)
        private const int WorkFactor = 12;

        /// <summary>
        /// Hash máš­t khášĐu bášąng BCrypt. Salt ngášŦu nhiÃŠn ÄÆ°áŧĢc tášĄo táŧą Äáŧng,
        /// nhÃšng vÃ o trong chuáŧi hash â khÃīng cáš§n lÆ°u salt riÃŠng.
        /// </summary>
        public static string Hash(string plainPassword)
            => BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.HashPassword(plainPassword, WorkFactor);

        /// <summary>
        /// XÃĄc minh máš­t khášĐu nháš­p vÃ o váŧi hash ÄÃĢ lÆ°u trong DB.
        /// BCrypt táŧą extract salt táŧŦ hash â truyáŧn vÃ o ÄÃšng 2 tham sáŧ lÃ  Äáŧ§.
        /// </summary>
        public static bool Verify(string plainPassword, string hashedPassword)
        {
            try
            {
                return BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.Verify(plainPassword, hashedPassword);
            }
            catch
            {
                // BášŊt trÆ°áŧng háŧĢp hash format cÅĐ (SHA-256) vášŦn cÃēn trong DB
                // â trášĢ false thay vÃŽ crash app
                return false;
            }
        }
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: ValidationHelper.cs ---
========================================

using System.Net.Mail;
using System.Text.RegularExpressions;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Táš­p trung toÃ n báŧ quy tášŊc validate dÃđng chung cho cÃĄc Service.
    /// Äáš·t 1 cháŧ Äáŧ khi thay Äáŧi quy tášŊc cháŧ sáŧ­a áŧ ÄÃĒy, ÃĄp dáŧĨng toÃ n app.
    /// </summary>
    public static class ValidationHelper
    {
        /// <summary>Máš­t khášĐu háŧĢp láŧ: táŧi thiáŧu 6 kÃ― táŧą, khÃīng cháŧ khoášĢng trášŊng.</summary>
        public static bool IsPasswordStrong(string password)
            => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(password) && password.Length >= 6;

        /// <summary>Email háŧĢp láŧ theo chuášĐn RFC (dÃđng MailAddress Äáŧ parse).</summary>
        public static bool IsValidEmail(string email)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(email)) return false;
            try
            {
                var addr = new MailAddress(email);
                return addr.Address == email.Trim();
            }
            catch { return false; }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Username háŧĢp láŧ: 3-50 kÃ― táŧą, cháŧ cháŧŊ cÃĄi, sáŧ vÃ  dášĨu gášĄch dÆ°áŧi.
        /// Regex: ^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{3,50}$
        /// </summary>
        public static bool IsValidUsername(string username)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(username)) return false;
            return Regex.IsMatch(username, @"^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{3,50}$");
        }
    }
}

========================================
--- FILE: IRepository.cs ---

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Generic repository interface â tášĨt cášĢ repository Äáŧu kášŋ tháŧŦa interface nÃ y.
    /// Ãp dáŧĨng Repository Pattern: tÃĄch biáŧt logic truy cáš­p dáŧŊ liáŧu kháŧi business logic.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">Kiáŧu entity (User, Project, TaskItem, ...)</typeparam>
    public interface IRepository<T> where T : class
    {
        /// <summary>LášĨy 1 bášĢn ghi theo khÃģa chÃ­nh. TrášĢ váŧ null nášŋu khÃīng tÃŽm thášĨy.</summary>
        Task<T?> GetByIdAsync(int id);

        /// <summary>LášĨy toÃ n báŧ danh sÃĄch. DÃđng GetPagedAsync nášŋu dáŧŊ liáŧu láŧn.</summary>
        Task<List<T>> GetAllAsync();

        /// <summary>ThÃŠm máŧi 1 bášĢn ghi vÃ o database.</summary>
        Task AddAsync(T entity);

        /// <summary>Cáš­p nháš­t 1 bášĢn ghi ÄÃĢ táŧn tášĄi.</summary>
        Task UpdateAsync(T entity);

        /// <summary>XÃģa bášĢn ghi theo ID (hard delete hoáš·c soft delete tÃđy repository).</summary>
        Task DeleteAsync(int id);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interface cho Authentication Service.
    /// Äáŧnh nghÄĐa contract â WinForms layer cháŧ biášŋt Interface nÃ y,
    /// khÃīng biášŋt cÃĄch implement bÃŠn trong.

    public interface IAuthService

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Auth
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triáŧn khai IAuthService â xÃĄc tháŧąc ngÆ°áŧi dÃđng (Login).
    ///
    /// Luáŧng ÄÄng nháš­p:
    ///   1. Validate username/password khÃīng ráŧng
    ///   2. TÃŽm user trong DB (cháŧ user active)
    ///   3. Verify BCrypt password qua PasswordHelper
    ///   4. Load danh sÃĄch Roles Äáŧ phÃĒn quyáŧn
    ///   5. Map User â UserSessionDto (khÃīng expose PasswordHash)
    ///   6. UpdateLastLogin fire-and-forget (khÃīng block UI)
    ///   7. TrášĢ LoginResult.Ok hoáš·c LoginResult.Fail
    ///
    /// DÃđng Result Pattern (LoginResult) thay vÃŽ throw Exception
    /// cho láŧi nghiáŧp váŧĨ â Form xáŧ­ lÃ― gáŧn hÆĄn, khÃīng cáš§n try-catch.
    /// </summary>
    public class AuthService : IAuthService
    {
        private readonly IUserRepository _userRepo;

        // Inject IUserRepository qua constructor (DI Container cung cášĨp)
        public AuthService(IUserRepository userRepo) => _userRepo = userRepo;

        public async Task<LoginResult> LoginAsync(string username, string password)
        {
            // --- BÆ°áŧc 1: Validate Äáš§u vÃ o (guard clauses) ---
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(username))
                return LoginResult.Fail("â  Vui lÃēng nháš­p tÃŠn ÄÄng nháš­p.");

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(password))
                return LoginResult.Fail("â  Vui lÃēng nháš­p máš­t khášĐu.");

            // --- BÆ°áŧc 2: TÃŽm user trong DB ---
            // GetByUsernameAsync cháŧ trášĢ user cÃģ IsActive = true
            var user = await _userRepo.GetByUsernameAsync(username.Trim());

            // --- BÆ°áŧc 3: Verify BCrypt password ---
            // DÃđng thÃīng bÃĄo chung cho cášĢ 2 trÆ°áŧng háŧĢp sai username / sai password
            // â trÃĄnh tiášŋt láŧ username cÃģ táŧn tášĄi trong háŧ tháŧng khÃīng (security)
            if (user == null || !PasswordHelper.Verify(password, user.PasswordHash))
                return LoginResult.Fail("â  TÃŠn ÄÄng nháš­p hoáš·c máš­t khášĐu khÃīng ÄÃšng.");

            // --- BÆ°áŧc 4: Load Roles Äáŧ phÃĒn quyáŧn (eager load) ---
            var userWithRoles = await _userRepo.GetWithRolesAsync(user.Id);
            if (userWithRoles == null)
                return LoginResult.Fail("â  KhÃīng tháŧ tášĢi thÃīng tin quyáŧn. Vui lÃēng tháŧ­ lášĄi.");

            // --- BÆ°áŧc 5: Map â DTO (khÃīng trášĢ User entity thÃī ra ngoÃ i Service) ---
            var dto = UserSessionMapper.ToDto(userWithRoles);

            // --- BÆ°áŧc 6: Cáš­p nháš­t LastLogin (fire-and-forget, khÃīng await) ---
            // _ = báŧ qua Task trášĢ váŧ, khÃīng block thread UI
            _ = _userRepo.UpdateLastLoginAsync(user.Id);

            return LoginResult.Ok(dto);
        }

        // Delegate sang PasswordHelper â AuthService khÃīng cháŧĐa BCrypt logic tráŧąc tiášŋp
        // NguyÃŠn tášŊc Single Responsibility: AuthService lo flow, PasswordHelper lo thuáš­t toÃĄn
        public string HashPassword(string plainPassword) => PasswordHelper.Hash(plainPassword);
        public bool VerifyPassword(string plain, string hashed) => PasswordHelper.Verify(plain, hashed);
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: UserSessionMapper.cs ---

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Auth
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Chuyáŧn Äáŧi User entity â UserSessionDto.
    ///
    /// TÃĄch ra file riÃŠng vÃŽ:
    ///   - AuthService khÃīng nÃŠn cháŧĐa mapping logic (Single Responsibility)
    ///   - Dáŧ tÃĄi dÃđng khi cáš§n refresh session sau nÃ y
    ///   - Dáŧ unit test mapping Äáŧc láš­p váŧi logic login
    ///
    /// UserSessionDto cháŧ cháŧĐa thÃīng tin cáš§n thiášŋt cho UI,
    /// Äáš·c biáŧt KHÃNG cÃģ PasswordHash â an toÃ n hÆĄn khi lÆ°u vÃ o AppSession.
    /// </summary>
    internal static class UserSessionMapper
    {
        internal static UserSessionDto ToDto(User user) => new()
        {
            Id         = user.Id,
            Username   = user.Username,
            FullName   = user.FullName,
            Email      = user.Email,
            AvatarPath = user.AvatarPath,
            // LášĨy tÃŠn cÃĄc Role táŧŦ navigation property UserRoles â Role
            // VÃ­ dáŧĨ kášŋt quášĢ: ["Admin"] hoáš·c ["Manager"] hoáš·c ["Developer"]
            Roles      = user.UserRoles?
                .Select(ur => ur.Role.Name)
                .ToList()
                ?? new List<string>()
        };
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Projects
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Nghiáŧp váŧĨ quášĢn lÃ― dáŧą ÃĄn: tášĄo/sáŧ­a/xÃģa dáŧą ÃĄn, Äáŧi trášĄng thÃĄi, quášĢn lÃ― thÃ nh viÃŠn.
    /// </summary>
    public class ProjectService : IProjectService
    {
        private readonly IProjectRepository _projectRepo;

        public ProjectService(IProjectRepository projectRepo)
            => _projectRepo = projectRepo;

        // Danh sÃĄch dáŧą ÃĄn theo quyáŧn
        public Task<List<Project>> GetProjectsForUserAsync(int userId, bool isManager)
            => isManager ? _projectRepo.GetAllAsync() : _projectRepo.GetByMemberAsync(userId);

        // Chi tiášŋt Äáš§y Äáŧ§
        public Task<Project?> GetProjectDetailsAsync(int projectId)
            => _projectRepo.GetWithDetailsAsync(projectId);

        // TášĄo dáŧą ÃĄn máŧi
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateProjectAsync(Project project)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(project.Name))
                return (false, "TÃŠn dáŧą ÃĄn khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧ tráŧng.");

            await _projectRepo.AddAsync(project);
            return (true, $"Dáŧą ÃĄn \"{project.Name}\" ÄÃĢ ÄÆ°áŧĢc tášĄo thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        // Cáš­p nháš­t dáŧą ÃĄn
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProjectAsync(Project project)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(project.Name))
                return (false, "TÃŠn dáŧą ÃĄn khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧ tráŧng.");

            await _projectRepo.UpdateAsync(project);
            return (true, "Cáš­p nháš­t dáŧą ÃĄn thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        // XÃģa dáŧą ÃĄn â kiáŧm tra cÃģ task chÆ°a
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteProjectAsync(int projectId)
        {
            if (await _projectRepo.HasTasksAsync(projectId))
                return (false, "KhÃīng tháŧ xÃģa dáŧą ÃĄn ÄÃĢ cÃģ cÃīng viáŧc. HÃĢy xÃģa cÃīng viáŧc trÆ°áŧc hoáš·c chuyáŧn trášĄng thÃĄi Cancelled.");

            await _projectRepo.DeleteAsync(projectId);
            return (true, "XÃģa dáŧą ÃĄn thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        // Äáŧi trášĄng thÃĄi dáŧą ÃĄn
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeStatusAsync(int projectId, string newStatus)
        {
            var validStatuses = new[] { "NotStarted", "InProgress", "OnHold", "Completed", "Cancelled" };
            if (!validStatuses.Contains(newStatus))
                return (false, $"TrášĄng thÃĄi \"{newStatus}\" khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ.");

            await _projectRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(projectId, newStatus);
            return (true, $"ÄÃĢ chuyáŧn trášĄng thÃĄi thÃ nh {newStatus}.");
        }

        // ââ QuášĢn lÃ― thÃ nh viÃŠn ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

        public Task<List<ProjectMember>> GetMembersAsync(int projectId)
            => _projectRepo.GetMembersAsync(projectId);

        // ThÃŠm thÃ nh viÃŠn â kiáŧm tra trÃđng
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AddMemberAsync(
            int projectId, int userId, string projectRole)
        {
            // Kiáŧm tra ÄÃĢ lÃ  thÃ nh viÃŠn chÆ°a
            var members = await _projectRepo.GetMembersAsync(projectId);
            if (members.Any(m => m.UserId == userId))
                return (false, "NgÆ°áŧi dÃđng ÄÃĢ lÃ  thÃ nh viÃŠn cáŧ§a dáŧą ÃĄn nÃ y.");

            var member = new ProjectMember
            {
                ProjectId   = projectId,
                UserId      = userId,
                ProjectRole = projectRole,
                JoinedAt    = DateTime.UtcNow
            };
            await _projectRepo.AddMemberAsync(member);
            return (true, "ThÃŠm thÃ nh viÃŠn thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        // XÃģa thÃ nh viÃŠn (soft delete: set LeftAt)
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> RemoveMemberAsync(int projectId, int userId)
        {
            await _projectRepo.RemoveMemberAsync(projectId, userId);
            return (true, "ÄÃĢ xÃģa thÃ nh viÃŠn kháŧi dáŧą ÃĄn.");
        }
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Constants;

// Namespace "Tasks" (sáŧ nhiáŧu) vÃŽ "Task" trÃđng System.Threading.Tasks.Task
namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Tasks
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triáŧn khai ITaskService cho GD4.
    ///
    /// THáŧ°C Tášū SEED DATA (LookupSeeder.cs â tháŧĐ táŧą insert = Id):
    ///   Roles:      Id=1 "Admin" | Id=2 "Manager" | Id=3 "Developer"
    ///   Statuses:   Id=1 "CREATED" | Id=2 "ASSIGNED" | Id=3 "IN-PROGRESS" | Id=4 "FAILED"
    ///               Id=5 "REVIEW-1" | Id=6 "REVIEW-2" | Id=7 "APPROVED" | Id=8 "IN-TEST"
    ///               Id=9 "RESOLVED" | Id=10 "CLOSED"
    ///   Priorities: Id=1 "Low" | Id=2 "Medium" | Id=3 "High" | Id=4 "Critical"
    ///
    /// PHÃN QUYáŧN UpdateStatusAsync:
    ///   Admin / Manager â báŧ qua workflow, Äáŧi sang BášĪT Káŧē status nÃ o
    ///   Developer       â cháŧ ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧi task ÄÆ°áŧĢc giao cho mÃŽnh (AssignedToId == UserId)
    ///
    /// SO SÃNH ROLE: dÃđng OrdinalIgnoreCase Äáŧ trÃĄnh láŧi casing
    ///   DB seed: "Admin", "Manager", "Developer" (hoa cháŧŊ cÃĄi Äáš§u)
    ///   AppSession.Roles cÃģ tháŧ cháŧĐa bášĨt káŧģ casing nÃ o â luÃīn dÃđng IgnoreCase
    /// </summary>
    public class TaskService : ITaskService
    {
        private readonly ITaskRepository _taskRepo;
        private readonly IUserRepository _userRepo;

        public TaskService(ITaskRepository taskRepo, IUserRepository userRepo)
        {
            _taskRepo = taskRepo ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(taskRepo));
            _userRepo = userRepo ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(userRepo));
        }

        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        // TRUY VášĪN â giáŧŊ nguyÃŠn 100%
        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

        public Task<TaskItem?> GetByIdAsync(int taskId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByIdWithDetailsAsync(taskId);

        public Task<(List<TaskItem> Items, int TotalCount)> GetPagedAsync(
            int page, int pageSize,
            int? projectId = null, int? assignedToId = null,
            int? statusId  = null, int? priorityId   = null,
            int? categoryId = null, string? keyword   = null)
            => _taskRepo.GetPagedAsync(page, pageSize,
                projectId, assignedToId, statusId, priorityId, categoryId, keyword);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetMyTasksAsync(int userId)
            => _taskRepo.GetAssignedToUserAsync(userId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForReviewer1Async(int reviewerId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByReviewer1Async(reviewerId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForReviewer2Async(int reviewerId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByReviewer2Async(reviewerId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForTesterAsync(int testerId)
            => _taskRepo.GetByTesterAsync(testerId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetOverdueTasksAsync()
            => _taskRepo.GetOverdueAsync();

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetDueSoonTasksAsync(int days = 7)
            => _taskRepo.GetDueSoonAsync(days);

        public Task<Dictionary<string, int>> GetStatusSummaryAsync(int projectId)
            => _taskRepo.GetStatusSummaryByProjectAsync(projectId);

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetAllByProjectAsync(int projectId)
        {
            return _taskRepo.GetByProjectAsync(projectId);
        }

        public Task<List<TaskItem>> GetBoardTasksAsync(int projectId)
        {
            return _taskRepo.GetByProjectAsync(projectId);
        }

        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        // CRUD
        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateTaskAsync(TaskItem task)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Title))
                return (false, "TiÃŠu Äáŧ cÃīng viáŧc khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧ tráŧng.");
            if (task.Title.Length > 200)
                return (false, "TiÃŠu Äáŧ khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc vÆ°áŧĢt quÃĄ 200 kÃ― táŧą.");
            if (task.ProjectId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃēng cháŧn dáŧą ÃĄn cho cÃīng viáŧc.");
            if (task.PriorityId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃēng cháŧn máŧĐc Äáŧ Æ°u tiÃŠn.");
            if (task.StatusId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃēng cháŧn trášĄng thÃĄi.");
            if (task.CategoryId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lÃēng cháŧn loášĄi cÃīng viáŧc.");
            if (task.EstimatedHours.HasValue && task.EstimatedHours.Value <= 0)
                return (false, "Sáŧ giáŧ Æ°áŧc tÃ­nh phášĢi láŧn hÆĄn 0.");
            if (task.DueDate.HasValue && task.DueDate.Value < DateTime.UtcNow.AddDays(-1))
                return (false, "HášĄn chÃģt khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc lÃ  ngÃ y trong quÃĄ kháŧĐ.");

            task.Title       = task.Title.Trim();
            task.Description = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Description)
                ? null : task.Description.Trim();

            await _taskRepo.AddAsync(task);
            return (true, $"ÄÃĢ tášĄo cÃīng viáŧc \"{task.Title}\" thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Cáš­p nháš­t task â gáŧi 2 method Repository riÃŠng biáŧt Äáŧ trÃĄnh EF tracking conflict:
        ///
        ///   1. UpdateAsync(task)
        ///      DÃđng Attach + State.Modified Äáŧ cáš­p nháš­t cÃĄc trÆ°áŧng náŧi dung
        ///      (Title, Description, AssignedToId, PriorityId, DueDate, v.v.)
        ///      Tuy nhiÃŠn khi entity load bášąng AsNoTracking cÃģ navigation property
        ///      (task.Status, task.Priority lÃ  object), EF ÄÃīi khi khÃīng ghi FK ÄÃšng.
        ///
        ///   2. UpdateStatusAsync(task.Id, task.StatusId)
        ///      DÃđng ExecuteUpdateAsync â sinh SQL "SET StatusId=? WHERE Id=?" tráŧąc tiášŋp,
        ///      khÃīng pháŧĨ thuáŧc vÃ o tracking state â ÄášĢm bášĢo StatusId luÃīn ÄÆ°áŧĢc ghi ÄÃšng.
        ///
        /// TÆ°ÆĄng táŧą: AssignedToId cÅĐng ÄÆ°áŧĢc UpdateAsync ghi ÄÃšng vÃŽ lÃ  FK thuáš§n (int?),
        /// khÃīng cÃģ navigation conflict pháŧĐc tášĄp nhÆ° StatusId.
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateTaskAsync(TaskItem task)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Title))
                return (false, "TiÃŠu Äáŧ cÃīng viáŧc khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧ tráŧng.");

            task.Title = task.Title.Trim();
            task.Description = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(task.Description) ? null : task.Description.Trim();

            try
            {
                await _taskRepo.UpdateAsync(task); // â Máŧt láš§n duy nhášĨt, ÄÃšng hoÃ n toÃ n
                return (true, "Cáš­p nháš­t cÃīng viáŧc thÃ nh cÃīng.");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, "Láŧi khi lÆ°u vÃ o Database: " + ex.Message);
            }
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteTaskAsync(int taskId)
        {
            var task = await _taskRepo.GetByIdWithDetailsAsync(taskId);
            if (task == null)
                return (false, "KhÃīng tÃŽm thášĨy cÃīng viáŧc.");
            if (task.SubTasks.Count > 0)
                return (false,
                    $"KhÃīng tháŧ xÃģa vÃŽ cÃīng viáŧc nÃ y cÃģ {task.SubTasks.Count} cÃīng viáŧc con. " +
                    "HÃĢy xÃģa cÃĄc cÃīng viáŧc con trÆ°áŧc.");

            await _taskRepo.DeleteAsync(taskId);
            return (true, $"ÄÃĢ xÃģa cÃīng viáŧc \"{task.Title}\".");
        }

        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        // CášŽP NHášŽT TIášūN Äáŧ
        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        
        private const int ResolvedStatusId = 9;
        private const int ClosedStatusId = 10;
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProgressAsync(
            int taskId, byte progress)
        {
            if (progress > 100)
                return (false, "Tiášŋn Äáŧ phášĢi táŧŦ 0 Äášŋn 100.");
            await _taskRepo.UpdateProgressAsync(taskId, progress, ResolvedStatusId);

            return progress == 100
                ? (true, "ð CÃīng viáŧc ÄÃĢ hoÃ n thÃ nh! TrášĄng thÃĄi chuyáŧn sang RESOLVED.")
                : (true, $"ÄÃĢ cáš­p nháš­t tiášŋn Äáŧ {progress}%.");
        }

        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        // CášŽP NHášŽT TRáš NG THÃI â PHÃN QUYáŧN LINH HOáš T
        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

        /// <summary>
        /// Chuyáŧn trášĄng thÃĄi workflow váŧi phÃĒn quyáŧn linh hoášĄt.
        ///
        /// PHÃN QUYáŧN:
        ///   Admin / Manager â ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧi sang BášĪT Káŧē trong 10 status, báŧ qua workflow.
        ///   Developer       â cháŧ ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧi task ÄÆ°áŧĢc giao cho mÃŽnh (AssignedToId == UserId).
        ///
        /// THAM Sáŧ statusId:
        ///   Truyáŧn Id tráŧąc tiášŋp táŧŦ ComboBox (KHÃNG dÃđng tÃŠn string) Äáŧ trÃĄnh láŧi
        ///   so kháŧp tÃŠn khi DB seed hoáš·c casing thay Äáŧi.
        ///
        /// SO SÃNH ROLE (quan tráŧng):
        ///   DB seed: "Admin", "Manager", "Developer"
        ///   AppSession.Roles: List&lt;string&gt; â dÃđng OrdinalIgnoreCase Äáŧ khÃīng láŧi
        ///   nášŋu source nÃ o ÄÃģ trášĢ váŧ "admin", "MANAGER", "developer"...
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateStatusAsync(
            int taskId, int statusId,
            int requesterId, IList<string> requesterRoles)
        {
            // Validate nhanh bášąng range (seed data: 1-10)
            if (statusId is < 1 or > 10)
                return (false, $"TrášĄng thÃĄi khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ (Id={statusId}). PhášĢi táŧŦ 1 Äášŋn 10.");

            // LášĨy tÃŠn status Äáŧ hiáŧn tháŧ message â cháŧ khi cáš§n (sau khi auth pass)
            bool isManagerOrAbove =
                requesterRoles.Any(r => r.Equals("Admin", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                                        r.Equals("Manager", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            if (isManagerOrAbove)
            {
                await _taskRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(taskId, statusId);
                return (true, $"ÄÃĢ chuyáŧn trášĄng thÃĄi sang \"{WorkflowConstants.GetStatusName(statusId)}\".");
            }

            var task = await _taskRepo.GetByIdAsync(taskId);
            if (task == null)
                return (false, "KhÃīng tÃŽm thášĨy cÃīng viáŧc.");

            if (task.AssignedToId != requesterId)
                return (false,
                    "BášĄn cháŧ cÃģ tháŧ thay Äáŧi trášĄng thÃĄi cÃīng viáŧc ÄÆ°áŧĢc giao cho mÃŽnh.\n" +
                    "LiÃŠn háŧ Manager nášŋu cáš§n thay Äáŧi task khÃĄc.");

            await _taskRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(taskId, statusId);
            return (true, $"ÄÃĢ chuyáŧn trášĄng thÃĄi sang \"{WorkflowConstants.GetStatusName(statusId)}\".");
        }

        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        // ASSIGN & TRANSITION
        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AssignAndTransitionAsync(
            int taskId, string newStatus,
            int? reviewer1Id = null, int? reviewer2Id = null, int? testerId = null)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(newStatus))
                return (false, "TÃŠn trášĄng thÃĄi khÃīng ÄÆ°áŧĢc Äáŧ tráŧng.");

            var statuses = await _taskRepo.GetAllStatusesAsync();
            // OrdinalIgnoreCase cho AssignAndTransition vÃŽ caller truyáŧn tÃŠn string
            var target   = statuses.FirstOrDefault(
                s => s.Name.Equals(newStatus, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));

            if (target == null)
                return (false, $"TrášĄng thÃĄi \"{newStatus}\" khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ.");

            var task = await _taskRepo.GetByIdAsync(taskId);
            if (task == null)
                return (false, "KhÃīng tÃŽm thášĨy cÃīng viáŧc.");

            if (reviewer1Id.HasValue)
            {
                if (reviewer1Id.Value <= 0)
                    return (false, "Reviewer láš§n 1 khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ.");
                var r1 = await _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(reviewer1Id.Value);
                if (r1 == null || !r1.IsActive)
                    return (false, $"Reviewer 1 (Id={reviewer1Id.Value}) khÃīng táŧn tášĄi hoáš·c ÄÃĢ báŧ khÃģa.");
            }

            if (reviewer2Id.HasValue)
            {
                if (reviewer2Id.Value <= 0)
                    return (false, "Reviewer láš§n 2 khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ.");
                var r2 = await _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(reviewer2Id.Value);
                if (r2 == null || !r2.IsActive)
                    return (false, $"Reviewer 2 (Id={reviewer2Id.Value}) khÃīng táŧn tášĄi hoáš·c ÄÃĢ báŧ khÃģa.");
            }

            if (testerId.HasValue)
            {
                if (testerId.Value <= 0)
                    return (false, "Tester khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ.");
                var t = await _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(testerId.Value);
                if (t == null || !t.IsActive)
                    return (false, $"Tester (Id={testerId.Value}) khÃīng táŧn tášĄi hoáš·c ÄÃĢ báŧ khÃģa.");
            }

            await _taskRepo.AssignReviewerAsync(
                taskId, reviewer1Id, reviewer2Id, testerId, target.Id);

            var parts = new List<string>();
            if (reviewer1Id.HasValue) parts.Add("Reviewer 1");
            if (reviewer2Id.HasValue) parts.Add("Reviewer 2");
            if (testerId.HasValue)    parts.Add("Tester");

            var extra = parts.Count > 0 ? $" â ÄÃĢ gÃĄn {string.Join(", ", parts)}" : string.Empty;
            return (true, $"Chuyáŧn sang {newStatus}{extra} thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
        // LOOKUP
        // ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

        public Task<List<Status>>   GetAllStatusesAsync()   => _taskRepo.GetAllStatusesAsync();
        public Task<List<Priority>> GetAllPrioritiesAsync() => _taskRepo.GetAllPrioritiesAsync();
        public Task<List<Category>> GetAllCategoriesAsync() => _taskRepo.GetAllCategoriesAsync();
    }
}

--- FILE: UserService.cs ---

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Users
{
    public class UserService : IUserService
    {
        private readonly IUserRepository _userRepo;
        private readonly IAuthService    _authService;

        public UserService(IUserRepository userRepo, IAuthService authService)
        {
            _userRepo    = userRepo;
            _authService = authService;
        }

        public Task<List<User>> GetAllUsersAsync()        => _userRepo.GetAllWithRolesAsync();
        public Task<List<User>> GetAllActiveUsersAsync()  => _userRepo.GetAllAsync();
        public Task<User?> GetByIdAsync(int id)           => _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(id);

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateUserAsync(
            string username, string fullName, string email, string password, string roleName, string? phone = null)
        {
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsValidUsername(username))
                return (false, "Username cháŧ gáŧm cháŧŊ, sáŧ, dášĨu gášĄch dÆ°áŧi (3â50 kÃ― táŧą).");
            if (await _userRepo.IsUsernameExistsAsync(username))
                return (false, $"Username '{username}' ÄÃĢ táŧn tášĄi.");
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsValidEmail(email))
                return (false, "Email khÃīng háŧĢp láŧ.");
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsPasswordStrong(password))
                return (false, "Máš­t khášĐu phášĢi cÃģ Ã­t nhášĨt 6 kÃ― táŧą.");

            var user = new User
            {
                Username     = username.Trim(),
                FullName     = fullName.Trim(),
                Email        = email.Trim(),
                Phone        = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(phone) ? null : phone.Trim(),
                PasswordHash = _authService.HashPassword(password),
                IsActive     = true
            };
            await _userRepo.AddWithRoleAsync(user, roleName);
            return (true, $"TášĄo tÃ i khoášĢn '{username}' thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateUserAsync(User user)
        {
            await _userRepo.UpdateAsync(user);
            return (true, "Cáš­p nháš­t thÃīng tin thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeactivateUserAsync(int userId)
        {
            await _userRepo.SetActiveAsync(userId, false);
            return (true, "TÃ i khoášĢn ÄÃĢ báŧ vÃī hiáŧu hÃģa.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ActivateUserAsync(int userId)
        {
            await _userRepo.SetActiveAsync(userId, true);
            return (true, "TÃ i khoášĢn ÄÃĢ ÄÆ°áŧĢc kÃ­ch hoášĄt lášĄi.");
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangePasswordAsync(
            int userId, string oldPassword, string newPassword)
        {
            var user = await _userRepo.GetByIdAsync(userId);
            if (user == null)
                return (false, "KhÃīng tÃŽm thášĨy tÃ i khoášĢn.");
            if (!_authService.VerifyPassword(oldPassword, user.PasswordHash))
                return (false, "Máš­t khášĐu cÅĐ khÃīng ÄÃšng.");
            if (!ValidationHelper.IsPasswordStrong(newPassword))
                return (false, "Máš­t khášĐu máŧi phášĢi cÃģ Ã­t nhášĨt 6 kÃ― táŧą.");

            await _userRepo.UpdatePasswordAsync(userId, _authService.HashPassword(newPassword));
            return (true, "Äáŧi máš­t khášĐu thÃ nh cÃīng.");
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Äáŧi vai trÃē cho user (cháŧ Admin gáŧi táŧŦ form).
        /// XÃģa tášĨt cášĢ role cÅĐ â gÃĄn role máŧi.
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeRoleAsync(int userId, string newRoleName)
        {
            try
            {
                await _userRepo.ChangeRoleAsync(userId, newRoleName);
                return (true, $"ÄÃĢ Äáŧi vai trÃē thÃ nh {newRoleName}.");
            }
            catch (InvalidOperationException ex)
            {
                return (false, ex.Message);
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, "Láŧi khi Äáŧi vai trÃē: " + (ex.InnerException?.Message ?? ex.Message));
            }
        }
    }
}

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Design;
using TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure
{
    public class DesignTimeDbContextFactory
        : IDesignTimeDbContextFactory<AppDbContext>
    {
        public AppDbContext CreateDbContext(string[] args)
        {
            var optionsBuilder = new DbContextOptionsBuilder<AppDbContext>();

            optionsBuilder.UseSqlServer(
                "Server=.\\SQLEXPRESS2022;Database=TaskFlowManagementDb;Trusted_Connection=True;TrustServerCertificate=True;"
            );

            return new AppDbContext(optionsBuilder.Options);
        }
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: AppDbContext.cs ---

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data
{
    /// <summary>
    /// AppDbContext â cáš§u náŧi giáŧŊa C# entities vÃ  SQL Server database.
    /// CášĨu hÃŽnh quan háŧ bášąng Fluent API trong OnModelCreating.
    /// 
    /// GD3: ThÃŠm relationships cho Reviewer1, Reviewer2, Tester trÃŠn TaskItem.
    /// </summary>
    public class AppDbContext : DbContext
    {
        // ââ DbSets: máŧi property = 1 bášĢng trong DB ââââââââââ
        public DbSet<User>          Users          { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Role>          Roles          { get; set; }
        public DbSet<UserRole>      UserRoles      { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Customer>      Customers      { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Project>       Projects       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<ProjectMember> ProjectMembers { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Expense>       Expenses       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Category>      Categories     { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Priority>      Priorities     { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Status>        Statuses       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<TaskItem>      TaskItems      { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Comment>       Comments       { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Attachment>    Attachments    { get; set; }
        public DbSet<Tag>           Tags           { get; set; }
        public DbSet<TaskTag>       TaskTags       { get; set; }

        public AppDbContext(DbContextOptions<AppDbContext> options) : base(options) { }

        protected override void OnModelCreating(ModelBuilder modelBuilder)
        {
            base.OnModelCreating(modelBuilder);

            // ââ Composite Keys ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<UserRole>()
                .HasKey(ur => new { ur.UserId, ur.RoleId });

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskTag>()
                .HasKey(tt => new { tt.TaskItemId, tt.TagId });

            // ââ User Relationships ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<UserRole>()
                .HasOne(ur => ur.User).WithMany(u => u.UserRoles)
                .HasForeignKey(ur => ur.UserId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<UserRole>()
                .HasOne(ur => ur.Role).WithMany(r => r.UserRoles)
                .HasForeignKey(ur => ur.RoleId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<User>()
                .HasIndex(u => u.Email).IsUnique();
            modelBuilder.Entity<User>()
                .HasIndex(u => u.Username).IsUnique();

            // ââ Project Relationships âââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .HasOne(p => p.Owner).WithMany(u => u.OwnedProjects)
                .HasForeignKey(p => p.OwnerId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .HasOne(p => p.Customer).WithMany(c => c.Projects)
                .HasForeignKey(p => p.CustomerId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.SetNull);

            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>()
                .HasOne(pm => pm.Project).WithMany(p => p.Members)
                .HasForeignKey(pm => pm.ProjectId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>()
                .HasOne(pm => pm.User).WithMany(u => u.ProjectMemberships)
                .HasForeignKey(pm => pm.UserId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>()
                .HasIndex(pm => new { pm.ProjectId, pm.UserId }).IsUnique();

            // ââ Task Relationships ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ

            // NgÆ°áŧi tášĄo task
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.CreatedBy).WithMany(u => u.CreatedTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.CreatedById)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // NgÆ°áŧi ÄÆ°áŧĢc giao tháŧąc hiáŧn
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.AssignedTo).WithMany(u => u.AssignedTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.AssignedToId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // GD3: Reviewer láš§n 1 (peer review)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.Reviewer1).WithMany(u => u.Review1Tasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.Reviewer1Id)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // GD3: Reviewer láš§n 2 (senior review)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.Reviewer2).WithMany(u => u.Review2Tasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.Reviewer2Id)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // GD3: Tester (QA)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.Tester).WithMany(u => u.TesterTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.TesterId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // Task cha â Task con (self-referencing)
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .HasOne(t => t.ParentTask).WithMany(t => t.SubTasks)
                .HasForeignKey(t => t.ParentTaskId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // ââ Expense Relationships âââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>()
                .HasOne(e => e.Project).WithMany(p => p.Expenses)
                .HasForeignKey(e => e.ProjectId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>()
                .HasOne(e => e.CreatedBy).WithMany(u => u.CreatedExpenses)
                .HasForeignKey(e => e.CreatedById)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            // ââ Attachment & Tag ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<Attachment>()
                .HasOne(a => a.UploadedBy).WithMany()
                .HasForeignKey(a => a.UploadedById)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskTag>()
                .HasOne(tt => tt.TaskItem).WithMany(t => t.TaskTags)
                .HasForeignKey(tt => tt.TaskItemId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskTag>()
                .HasOne(tt => tt.Tag).WithMany(t => t.TaskTags)
                .HasForeignKey(tt => tt.TagId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            // ââ Indexes âââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.ProjectId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_ProjectId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.StatusId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_StatusId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.PriorityId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_PriorityId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.AssignedToId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_AssignedToId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.DueDate).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_DueDate");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.CreatedAt).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_CreatedAt");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => new { t.ProjectId, t.StatusId }).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_ProjectId_StatusId");

            // GD3: Index cho Reviewer/Tester queries
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.Reviewer1Id).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_Reviewer1Id");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.Reviewer2Id).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_Reviewer2Id");
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>().HasIndex(t => t.TesterId).HasDatabaseName("IX_TaskItems_TesterId");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>().HasIndex(p => p.OwnerId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Projects_OwnerId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>().HasIndex(p => p.Status).HasDatabaseName("IX_Projects_Status");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>().HasIndex(p => p.CustomerId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Projects_CustomerId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Comment>().HasIndex(c => c.TaskItemId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Comments_TaskItemId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>().HasIndex(e => e.ProjectId).HasDatabaseName("IX_Expenses_ProjectId");
            modelBuilder.Entity<ProjectMember>().HasIndex(pm => pm.UserId).HasDatabaseName("IX_ProjectMembers_UserId");

            // ProgressPercent: BYTE nÃŠn táŧi Äa 255 nhÆ°ng business rule lÃ  0-100
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_TaskItems_ProgressPercent",
                    "[ProgressPercent] BETWEEN 0 AND 100"));

            // EstimatedHours & ActualHours phášĢi dÆ°ÆĄng nášŋu cÃģ
            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_TaskItems_EstimatedHours",
                    "[EstimatedHours] IS NULL OR [EstimatedHours] > 0"));

            modelBuilder.Entity<TaskItem>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_TaskItems_ActualHours",
                    "[ActualHours] IS NULL OR [ActualHours] > 0"));

            // Expense.Amount phášĢi dÆ°ÆĄng
            modelBuilder.Entity<Expense>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_Expenses_Amount",
                    "[Amount] > 0"));

            // Project.Budget khÃīng ÃĒm
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_Projects_Budget",
                    "[Budget] >= 0"));

            // Project.Priority cháŧ 1-4
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_Projects_Priority",
                    "[Priority] BETWEEN 1 AND 4"));

            // Project.Status cháŧ ÄÆ°áŧĢc lÃ  cÃĄc giÃĄ tráŧ Äáŧnh nghÄĐa sášĩn
            modelBuilder.Entity<Project>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_Projects_Status",
                    "[Status] IN ('NotStarted','InProgress','OnHold','Completed','Cancelled')"));

            // Priority.Level cháŧ 1-4
            modelBuilder.Entity<Priority>()
                .ToTable(tb => tb.HasCheckConstraint(
                    "CK_Priorities_Level",
                    "[Level] BETWEEN 1 AND 4"));

            modelBuilder.Entity<Status>()
           .HasIndex(s => s.Name).IsUnique()
           .HasDatabaseName("UQ_Statuses_Name");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Status>()
                .HasIndex(s => s.DisplayOrder).IsUnique()
                .HasDatabaseName("UQ_Statuses_DisplayOrder");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Category>()
                .HasIndex(c => c.Name).IsUnique()
                .HasDatabaseName("UQ_Categories_Name");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Priority>()
                .HasIndex(p => p.Name).IsUnique()
                .HasDatabaseName("UQ_Priorities_Name");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Priority>()
                .HasIndex(p => p.Level).IsUnique()
                .HasDatabaseName("UQ_Priorities_Level");

            modelBuilder.Entity<Role>()
                .HasIndex(r => r.Name).IsUnique()
                .HasDatabaseName("UQ_Roles_Name");

            // âââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            // MáŧĨc 8: DeleteBehavior cho Attachment & Comment
            // âââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
            modelBuilder.Entity<Attachment>()
                .HasOne(a => a.TaskItem).WithMany(t => t.Attachments)
                .HasForeignKey(a => a.TaskItemId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<Comment>()
                .HasOne(c => c.TaskItem).WithMany(t => t.Comments)
                .HasForeignKey(c => c.TaskItemId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Cascade);

            modelBuilder.Entity<Comment>()
                .HasOne(c => c.User).WithMany(u => u.Comments)
                .HasForeignKey(c => c.UserId)
                .OnDelete(DeleteBehavior.Restrict);
            

        }
    }
}

--- FILE: DbSeeder.cs ---

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data.Seed;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Orchestrator seed data â gáŧi cÃĄc Seeder nháŧ theo ÄÃšng tháŧĐ táŧą FK.
    ///
    /// THáŧĻ Táŧ° BášŪT BUáŧC (do Foreign Key):
    ///   1. Lookup tables (Roles, Priorities, Statuses, Categories, Tags)
    ///   2. Users
    ///   3. UserRoles (cáš§n UserId + RoleId)
    ///   4. Customers
    ///   5. Projects (cáš§n UserId + CustomerId)
    ///   6. ProjectMembers (cáš§n ProjectId + UserId)
    ///   7. TaskItems (cáš§n ProjectId + UserId + StatusId + PriorityId + CategoryId)
    ///
    /// ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
    /// â ïļ  KHI NÃO CášĶN RESET DATABASE?
    ///
    ///   Nášŋu trÆ°áŧc ÄÃĒy chášĄy version dÃđng SHA-256 (hash cÅĐ),
    ///   DB Äang cÃģ hash sai format â login sáš― bÃĄo sai máš­t khášĐu.
    ///
    ///   CÃCH RESET (cháŧn 1 trong 3):
    ///
    ///   [A] SQL Server Management Studio (SSMS):
    ///       Kášŋt náŧi â chuáŧt phášĢi TaskFlowManagementDb â Delete â OK
    ///
    ///   [B] Package Manager Console (Visual Studio):
    ///       Tools â NuGet Package Manager â Package Manager Console
    ///       Cháŧn Default project: TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure
    ///       GÃĩ láŧnh:
    ///           Drop-Database
    ///       XÃĄc nháš­n Y â Enter
    ///
    ///   [C] Terminal / CMD:
    ///       cd TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure
    ///       dotnet ef database drop --force
    ///
    ///   Sau khi drop â chášĄy lášĄi app â DB táŧą tášĄo máŧi + seed BCrypt.
    /// ââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââââ
    /// </summary>
    public static class DbSeeder
    {
        public static async Task SeedAsync(AppDbContext context)
        {
            // Guard: cháŧ seed khi DB hoÃ n toÃ n tráŧng
            // Nášŋu ÄÃĢ cÃģ user â báŧ qua toÃ n báŧ (idempotent)
            if (await context.Users.AnyAsync()) return;

            // =====================================================
            // BÆŊáŧC 1: LOOKUP TABLES
            // PhášĢi commit trÆ°áŧc Äáŧ cÃģ ID cho cÃĄc bášĢng pháŧĨ thuáŧc
            // =====================================================
            var roles      = LookupSeeder.GetRoles();
            var priorities = LookupSeeder.GetPriorities();
            var statuses   = LookupSeeder.GetStatuses();
            var categories = LookupSeeder.GetCategories();
            var tags       = LookupSeeder.GetTags();

            context.AddRange(roles);
            context.AddRange(priorities);
            context.AddRange(statuses);
            context.AddRange(categories);
            context.AddRange(tags);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();
            // Sau SaveChanges: roles[0].Id, priorities[0].Id, ... ÄÃĢ cÃģ giÃĄ tráŧ táŧŦ DB

            // =====================================================
            // BÆŊáŧC 2: USERS (password hash bášąng BCrypt â xem SeedHelper)
            // =====================================================
            var users = UserSeeder.GetUsers();
            context.AddRange(users);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();
            // Sau ÄÃĒy users[i].Id ÄÃĢ cÃģ giÃĄ tráŧ

            // =====================================================
            // BÆŊáŧC 3: USER ROLES â gÃĄn quyáŧn theo username pattern
            // =====================================================
            var adminRole   = roles.First(r => r.Name == "Admin");
            var managerRole = roles.First(r => r.Name == "Manager");
            var devRole     = roles.First(r => r.Name == "Developer");

            var userRoles = users.Select(u => new UserRole
            {
                UserId = u.Id,
                RoleId = u.Username switch
                {
                    "admin"                              => adminRole.Id,
                    var n when n.StartsWith("manager")  => managerRole.Id,
                    _                                   => devRole.Id
                }
            }).ToList();

            context.AddRange(userRoles);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            // =====================================================
            // BÆŊáŧC 4: CUSTOMERS + PROJECTS
            // =====================================================
            var customers = ProjectSeeder.GetCustomers();
            context.AddRange(customers);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            var projects = ProjectSeeder.GetProjects(users, customers);
            context.AddRange(projects);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            // =====================================================
            // BÆŊáŧC 5: PROJECT MEMBERS â máŧi project 3-5 devs ngášŦu nhiÃŠn
            // =====================================================
            var devUsers = users.Where(u => u.Username.StartsWith("dev")).ToList();
            var rng      = new Random(42); // seed cáŧ Äáŧnh â reproducible

            var members = new List<ProjectMember>();
            foreach (var project in projects)
            {
                var assigned = devUsers
                    .OrderBy(_ => rng.Next())
                    .Take(rng.Next(3, 6))
                    .ToList();

                members.AddRange(assigned.Select(dev => new ProjectMember
                {
                    ProjectId   = project.Id,
                    UserId      = dev.Id,
                    ProjectRole = "Developer",
                    JoinedAt    = project.CreatedAt
                }));
            }
            context.AddRange(members);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();

            // =====================================================
            // BÆŊáŧC 6: TASK ITEMS â 10 task mášŦu máŧi project
            // =====================================================
            var taskList = BuildTaskItems(
                projects, members, users, priorities, statuses, categories, rng);

            context.AddRange(taskList);
            await context.SaveChangesAsync();
        }

        // -------------------------------------------------------
        // TÃĄch logic tášĄo task ra method riÃŠng cho gáŧn
        // -------------------------------------------------------
        private static List<TaskItem> BuildTaskItems(
            List<Project>       projects,
            List<ProjectMember> members,
            List<User>          users,
            List<Priority>      priorities,
            List<Status>        statuses,
            List<Category>      categories,
            Random              rng)
        {
            var now = DateTime.UtcNow;

            // Template (title, category, priority)
            var templates = new[]
            {
                ("PhÃĒn tÃ­ch yÃŠu cáš§u háŧ tháŧng",     "Feature",     "High"),
                ("Thiášŋt kášŋ database schema",         "Feature",     "High"),
                ("CÃ i Äáš·t mÃīi trÆ°áŧng development",   "Feature",     "Medium"),
                ("XÃĒy dáŧąng module xÃĄc tháŧąc Login",   "Feature",     "Critical"),
                ("API quášĢn lÃ― ngÆ°áŧi dÃđng",           "Feature",     "High"),
                ("UI Dashboard táŧng quan",           "Feature",     "Medium"),
                ("Fix bug phÃĒn quyáŧn sai",           "Bug",         "High"),
                ("Viášŋt unit test Auth module",       "Testing",     "Medium"),
                ("Táŧi Æ°u query performance",         "Improvement", "Medium"),
                ("Review code Pull Request #12",     "Research",    "Low"),
            };

            var result = new List<TaskItem>();

            foreach (var project in projects)
            {
                var projectDevs = members
                    .Where(m => m.ProjectId == project.Id)
                    .Select(m => users.First(u => u.Id == m.UserId))
                    .ToList();

                var owner = users.First(u => u.Id == project.OwnerId);

                for (int i = 0; i < templates.Length; i++)
                {
                    var (title, catName, priName) = templates[i];
                    var priority = priorities.First(p => p.Name == priName);
                    var status   = statuses[rng.Next(statuses.Count)];
                    var category = categories.FirstOrDefault(c => c.Name == catName)
                                   ?? categories.First();
                    var assignee = projectDevs.Count > 0
                        ? projectDevs[i % projectDevs.Count]
                        : owner;

                    var progress = status.Name == "Done"       ? (byte)100
                                 : status.Name == "InProgress" ? (byte)rng.Next(20, 80)
                                 : (byte)0;

                    result.Add(new TaskItem
                    {
                        Title           = title,
                        Description     = $"[{project.Name}] {title}",
                        ProjectId       = project.Id,
                        CreatedById     = owner.Id,
                        AssignedToId    = assignee.Id,
                        PriorityId      = priority.Id,
                        StatusId        = status.Id,
                        CategoryId      = category.Id,
                        DueDate         = now.AddDays(rng.Next(-7, 30)),
                        ProgressPercent = progress,
                        IsCompleted     = progress == 100,
                        EstimatedHours  = rng.Next(2, 20),
                        CreatedAt       = project.CreatedAt.AddDays(rng.Next(0, 10)),
                        UpdatedAt       = now,
                        CompletedAt     = progress == 100
                                          ? now.AddDays(-rng.Next(1, 7))
                                          : null
                    });
                }
            }

            return result;
        }
    }
}

using BCrypt.Net;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data.Seed
{
    /// <summary>
    /// HÃ m tiáŧn Ã­ch dÃđng chung cho toÃ n báŧ Seeder.
    /// TÃĄch riÃŠng Äáŧ trÃĄnh láš·p code vÃ  dáŧ thay Äáŧi thuáš­t toÃĄn hash sau nÃ y.
    /// </summary>
    internal static class SeedHelper
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Hash máš­t khášĐu bášąng BCrypt WorkFactor 12.
        ///
        /// â ïļ FIX: PhiÃŠn bášĢn cÅĐ dÃđng SHA-256 + Salt tÄĐnh.
        /// PhiÃŠn bášĢn nÃ y ÄÃĢ chuyáŧn sang BCrypt â salt táŧą Äáŧng, khÃĄc nhau máŧi láš§n hash.
        ///
        /// NášūU Báš N ÄÃ TáŧŠNG CHáš Y VERSION CÅĻ (SHA-256):
        ///   PhášĢi xÃģa DB cÅĐ trÆ°áŧc: DROP DATABASE TaskFlowManagementDb
        ///   Sau ÄÃģ chášĄy lášĄi app Äáŧ seed bášąng BCrypt.
        /// </summary>
        internal static string Hash(string password)
            => BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.HashPassword(password, workFactor: 12);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data.Seed
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Seed dáŧŊ liáŧu ngÆ°áŧi dÃđng máš·c Äáŧnh.
    ///
    /// Máš­t khášĐu ÄÆ°áŧĢc hash bášąng BCrypt (WorkFactor 12).

using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Data;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Infrastructure.Repositories
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triáŧn khai ICustomerRepository â thao tÃĄc dáŧŊ liáŧu cho Customer (KhÃĄch hÃ ng).
    /// </summary>
    public class CustomerRepository : ICustomerRepository
    {
        private readonly IDbContextFactory<AppDbContext> _contextFactory;

        public CustomerRepository(IDbContextFactory<AppDbContext> contextFactory)
            => _contextFactory = contextFactory;

        public async Task<Customer?> GetByIdAsync(int id)
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            return await ctx.Customers.AsNoTracking().FirstOrDefaultAsync(c => c.Id == id);
        }

        // Danh sÃĄch khÃĄch hÃ ng, sášŊp xášŋp A-Z theo tÃŠn cÃīng ty
        public async Task<List<Customer>> GetAllAsync()
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            return await ctx.Customers.AsNoTracking().OrderBy(c => c.CompanyName).ToListAsync();
        }

        // -------------------------------------------------------
        // TÃŽm kiášŋm full-text ÄÆĄn giášĢn trÃŠn 3 cáŧt
        // Contains â sinh ra SQL: WHERE CompanyName LIKE '%keyword%'
        // Nullable check trÆ°áŧc khi Contains Äáŧ trÃĄnh NullReferenceException
        // -------------------------------------------------------
        public async Task<List<Customer>> SearchAsync(string keyword)
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            return await ctx.Customers
                .AsNoTracking()
                .Where(c => c.CompanyName.Contains(keyword)
                         || (c.ContactName != null && c.ContactName.Contains(keyword))
                         || (c.Email       != null && c.Email.Contains(keyword)))
                .OrderBy(c => c.CompanyName)
                .ToListAsync();
        }

        // -------------------------------------------------------
        // LášĨy khÃĄch hÃ ng kÃĻm danh sÃĄch dáŧą ÃĄn (dÃđng cho form chi tiášŋt)
        // ThenInclude Owner Äáŧ hiáŧn tháŧ PM cáŧ§a táŧŦng dáŧą ÃĄn
        // -------------------------------------------------------
        public async Task<Customer?> GetWithProjectsAsync(int customerId)
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            return await ctx.Customers
                .AsNoTracking()
                .Include(c => c.Projects).ThenInclude(p => p.Owner)
                .FirstOrDefaultAsync(c => c.Id == customerId);
        }

        public async Task AddAsync(Customer customer)
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            customer.CreatedAt = DateTime.UtcNow;
            await ctx.Customers.AddAsync(customer);
            await ctx.SaveChangesAsync();
        }

        // Cáš­p nháš­t thÃīng tin khÃĄch hÃ ng, bášĢo váŧ CreatedAt
        public async Task UpdateAsync(Customer customer)
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            ctx.Customers.Attach(customer);
            ctx.Entry(customer).State = EntityState.Modified;
            ctx.Entry(customer).Property(c => c.CreatedAt).IsModified = false;
            await ctx.SaveChangesAsync();
        }

        // Hard delete â cÃģ tháŧ Äáŧi thÃ nh soft delete nášŋu cáš§n giáŧŊ láŧch sáŧ­
        public async Task DeleteAsync(int id)
        {
            using var ctx = _contextFactory.CreateDbContext();
            await ctx.Customers.Where(c => c.Id == id).ExecuteDeleteAsync();
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: ProjectRepository.cs ---
